The Indian batsmen again made a shaky performance, which Pakistan took full advantage of and won 85 runs on Thursday in the second one-day international cricket match to take an unassailable 2-0 lead in the three-match series
 pakistani team ne bharat ko khel ke har kshetra main kamjor sabit kiya
 Nasir Jamshed scored a century in adversity, while Junaid Khan, Umar Gul and Saeed Ajmal gave their team the best bowling with 12 balls remaining
 pakistan ne is tarah se eden gardens par apana ajey abhiyaan barkaraar rakhkar chauthi baar bhartiya sarajameen par shrunkhlaa jiti
 The sky was clouded
 mahendra singh dhoni ne toss jitkar pakistan ko pehle ballebaaji ke liye aamantrit karne main der nahin lagaai
 Jamshed scored a brilliant innings of 106 runs in 126 balls with the help of 12 fours and two sixes
 unhone mohammad hafeez (76) ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 141 ran kii saajhedaari kii lekin madhyakram ladkadaane se pakistani team 48
 He was dismissed for 250 in 3 overs
 eden gardens kii paristhitiyon main yah score mushkil nahin lag rahaa tha lekin bharat ke sheersh ballebaajon ke pakistani gendbaajon ke saamne natmastak hone se yah score bhi pahaad jaisaa ban gaya
 Dhoni (54 not out off 89 balls) was able to face the bowlers firmly but he did not get support from the other end
 bhartiya team 48 over main 165 ran par dher ho gai
 India will now play in the last match in Delhi on January 6 to save the happiness left
 pakistan kii taraf se ajmal or junayd ne teen-teen jabaki gul ne do wicket liye
 Virender Sehwag (31) and Gautam Gambhir (11) had trouble facing the balls of Junaid and Mohammad Irfan
 donon junayd kii seem or swing leti gendon se jujh rahe the jabaki irfan ne apane bousanr se unki acchhee pariksha lee
 Gambhir struggled from the start and in the tenth over of the innings, Junaid's ball hit the wicket with his bat
 iske baad viraat kohli (chah), sahvaag (31) or yuvaraj singh (nau) ne bhi darshakon ko niraash karne main der nahin lagaai
 Kohli teased the ball going towards the leg side in the next over of Junaid and Kamran Akmal dived to his left and gave India another blow with a beautiful catch
 umr gul 13wein over main pehle badlaav ke rup main aae or sahvaag or yuvaraj singh (nau) ko out karke bharat ko karaare jatke die
 When Sehwag lbw, Yuvraj catches the back of the wicket in an attempt to pull the short pitch ball
 suresh raina ne 42 gend par 18 ran banaae
 Akmal stumped out Raina and later Ravichandran Ashwin to ensure Pakistan's victory
 aswin ko ravinder jadeja se upar ballebaaji ke liye bheja gaya tha
 Ajmal completed the right spell by dismissing three wickets (jadeja, Bhuvneshwar Kumar and Ashok Dinda) in his one over
 dhoni ne junayd par pehle chakka or unke agle over main teen chauke jadkar vanade main 47waan ardhshtak puraa kiya
 This fast bowler ended the Indian innings by dismissing Ishant Sharma in this over
 isse pehle spinner jadeja (41 ran dekar teen wicket) or tej gendbaaj eshanth (34 ran dekar teen wicket) kii acchhee gendbaaji se bharat ne naatakeey vaapasi kii thi
 Pakistan got off to a good start after being invited to bat first
 hafeez or jamshed ko bhartiya tej gendbaajon ko khilne main kisi tarah kii pareshaani nahin hui
 Young bowlers like Dinda and Bhuvneshwar could not take advantage of favorable conditions as captain Dhoni thought after winning the toss
 duusari taraf pakistani salaami jodi ne chaturaai se ballebaaji karke pehle powerple ke lagbhag har over main gend ko seemaa rekha ke darshan karaae
 Playing the first match at his home ground, Dinda did several bouncers, three of which were called wide
 bhubaneshwar main bhi kisi tarah kaa painaapan nahin dikhaa
 Meanwhile, fielding was also not good, which made the job of Pakistani pair easy
 tippaniyan Hafeez completed his 150th half-century off 50 balls
 iske do over baad jamshed bhi is mukaam par pahunch gaye
 Part-time spinner Jadeja finally broke the partnership by bowling Hafeez
 ajahar ali (2) kaa kharaab farm jari rahaa or vah ran out hokar pavilion laut gaye
 Younis Khan (10) was given LBW out while the ball was on the pad touching his bat
 jamshed ne haalanki ek chor sanbhale rakhaa or apana teesraa shatak puraa kiya
 He has hit all three centuries against India
 vah aakhir tak krij par tike rahane main naakaam rahe or jadeja ke duusare shikaar bane
 Jadeja dismissed Akmal (naught) in the same over after which Ishant did not take long to bowl the tail batsmen

 For Pakistan, Ajmal and Junaid took three each while Gul took two wickets
 virendra sahvaag (31) or gautam gambhir (11) ko junayd or mohammad irfan kii gendon kaa saamana karne main pareshaani ai
 Both were struggling with Junaid's seam and swinging balls, while Irfan tested him well with his bouncer
 gambhir shuru se sangharsh kar rahe the or pari ke dasven over main junayd kii gend unke balle se lagakar wicket main ghus gai
 After this, Virat Kohli (six), Sehwag (31) and Yuvraj Singh (nine) also did not delay to disappoint the audience
 kohli ne junayd ke agle over main leg said kii taraf ja rahi gend ko chhedaa or kamran akmal ne apni bain taraf dive lagaakar khubasurat kaich se bharat ko doosraa jhatka diya
 Umar Gul came in as the first change in the 13th over and bowled India hard by dismissing Sehwag and Yuvraj Singh (nine)
 sahvaag elbeadblyoo out hue to yuvaraj ne short pich gend pul karne ke prayaas main wicket ke peeche kaich thamaya
 Suresh Raina scored 18 off 42 balls
 akmal ne pehle raina or baad main ravichandran aswin ko stump out karke pakistan kii jeet sunishchit kar di
 Ashwin was sent to bat above Ravinder Jadeja
 ajmal ne apane ek over main teen wicket (jadeja, bhubaneshwar kumaar or ashok dinda) ko out karke rahi sahi kasar puri kii
 Dhoni completed his 47th half-century in odis by hitting the first six over Junaid and three fours in his next over
 is tej gendbaaj ne isi over main eshanth sharma ko out karke bhartiya pari kaa ant kiya
 Earlier, India made a dramatic comeback with good bowling by spinner Jadeja (3 for 41) and fast bowler Ishant (3 for 34)
 pakistan ne pehle ballebaaji kaa nyauta milane par acchhee shuruyaat kii
 Hafeez and Jamshed had no problem playing the Indian fast bowlers
 dinda or bhubaneshwar jaise yuva gendbaaj anukool paristhitiyon kaa phayda nahin uthaa paae jaisaa ki captain dhoni ne toss jeetne ke baad sochaa tha
 The Pakistani opening pair, on the other hand, batted smartly and brought the ball to the boundary line in almost every over of the first powerplay
 apane gharelu maidan par pehla match khel rahe dinda kai bounsar kiye jinamein se teen ko wide qaraar diya
 Even in Bhubaneshwar, there was no sharpening
 is bich kshetrarakshan bhi acha nahin rahaa jisase pakistani jodi kaa kaam aasaan ho gaya

 Two overs later, Jamshed also reached this point
 part time spinner jadeja ne aakhir main hafeez ko bold karke yah saajhedaari todi
 Azhar Ali (2) continued in poor form and he was run out and returned to the pavilion
 younis khan (10) ko elbeadblyoo out diya gaya jabaki gend unke balle ko sparsh karke pad par lagi thi
 Jamshed however held one end and completed his third century
 unhone apane teenon shatak bharat ke khilaaf lagaae hai

 Chandrapur Lok Sabha comes under 6 assembly seats
 isamen rajura, chandrapur, ballarpur, varora, wani or arni vidhansabha seat shaamil hai
 While Rajura, Chandrapur, Ballarpur, Vani and Arni are occupied by the BJP, Warora is dominated by the Shiv Sena
